PUBLIC NOTICE
NOTICE OF DISSOLUTION OF UNREGISTERED FIRM
[Under Sec. 72(b) of the Partnership Act, 1932]
It is hereby informed to the General Public that the unregistered Partnership firm namely “M/s. Faruuzi”, which carried
on Restaurant Business at New No. 123, GST Road, Pallavaram, Chennai-600 043, has been dissolved with effect
from 21-11-2016.
Chennai,
27th April 2017.

FIROS C.M.
Partner of Dissolved Firm
